href="http://floridagunclassifieds.com/facebook-closes-gun-groups/" title="Facebook Closes Gun Groups: An open letter to facebook and Shannon Watts of Moms Demand Action For Gun Sense in America">Facebook Closes Gun Groups: An open letter to facebook and Shannon Watts of Moms Demand Action For Gun Sense in America</a></h3> <p class="meta dotted"><span class="dashicons-before user"><a href="http://floridagunclassifieds.com/author/matt-adika/" title="Posts by Matt Adika" rel="author">Matt Adika</a></span> <span class="dashicons-before folderb"><a href="http://floridagunclassifieds.com/category/firearms-blog/" rel="category tag">Firearms Blog</a></span> <span class="dashicons-before clock"><span>February 6, 2016</span></span></p> <div class="entry-content"> <img width="150" height="130" src="http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/facebook-closes-gun-groups-1.png?fit=150%2C130" class="attachment-blog-thumbnail size-blog-thumbnail wp-post-image" alt="facebook-closes-gun-groups" srcset="http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/facebook-closes-gun-groups-1.png?w=785 785w, http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/facebook-closes-gun-groups-1.png?resize=50%2C43 50w, http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/facebook-closes-gun-groups-1.png?resize=173%2C150 173w, http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/facebook-closes-gun-groups-1.png?resize=768%2C665 768w, http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/facebook-closes-gun-groups-1.png?resize=500%2C433 500w, http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/facebook-closes-gun-groups-1.png?resize=100%2C87 100w, http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/facebook-closes-gun-groups-1.png?resize=150%2C130 150w" sizes="(max-width: 150px) 100vw, 150px"> <h1 style="font-size: 175%; text-align: left;">Facebook Closes Gun Groups</h1> <p style="font-size: 175%; text-align: left;">An open letter from Matt Adika of Florida Gun Classifieds to facebook and Shannon Watts of Moms Demand Action For Gun Sense in America</p> <p style="font-size: 125%; text-align: left;"><strong>Dear Mrs Watts and Facebook executives,</strong></p> <p style="font-size: 125%; text-align: left;">I read your interview with Fast Company where you made a comment about how licensed dealers do not sell on Facebook and how Facebook Closes Gun Groups will solve the problem of the groups being&nbsp;plagued with criminals buying and selling firearms illegally. I have to say as a licensed FFL dealer, the owner of Florida Gun Classifieds <a href="http://floridagunclassifieds.com">http://floridagunclassifieds.com</a> which allows users to post ads to buy and sell firearms online, and the administrator of one of Florida’s best gun groups on Facebook, Florida Gun Classifieds,&nbsp;<em><strong>you do not have a clue of what you are talking about</strong></em> or what you have done by closing these groups.</p> <h2 style="font-size: 100%; text-align: left;">My excellent reputation in Florida is primarily because of Facebook, I have built my entire marketing campaign around Facebook and the gun groups that were hosted on Facebook. &nbsp;I was able to start from nothing at thirty years old to become one of the nation’s largest specialty dealers for high-end firearms within a few years because of the opportunity and reach of Facebook. Now that Facebook and your organization have pushed Facebook Closes Gun Groups,&nbsp;what you are&nbsp;essentially doing is killing the opportunity for small firearms dealers like myself to market directly to law-abiding consumers in their geographical area, and around the country.</h2> <h3 style="font-size: 100%; text-align: left;">You are also removing a significant tool which allows law enforcement and the ATF to find criminals who are buying and selling guns illegally. This eliminates the&nbsp;opportunity law enforcement has to gain electronic evidence of the criminal transfer of firearms. Just like with the sale and trafficking of illegal drugs, (which by the way is illegal yet still dominates the black market in every city in America). The “common sense approach” you have chosen to implement is only going to force the market to go underground and out of the scrutiny&nbsp;of watchful eyes. Not only does law enforcement monitor these groups, but many group administrators such as myself carefully screen all members before allowing them to join our groups.</h3> <p>All these groups have strict policies in place, and those policies which were strictly enforced, such as:</p> <ol> <li>No under age members permitted</li> <li>Anyone who looks like a “thug” prohibited</li> <li>Anyone who has pictures of illegal drugs or other illegal activities on their profile was also prohibited</li> </ol> <p>These people were never allowed into our groups. And when it was discovered that someone prohibited had&nbsp;slipped in, or that someone who was prohibited from buying or selling was trying to do so (illegally), they were banned from the group, and other administrators were notified and actively shared this information with their peers. We policed ourselves to keep our groups free of illegal activity. Keeping our groups free of illegal activity is obviously in our best interest. We are also advocates of obeying the law! Do you really think we want criminals obtaining firearms? HELL NO! Criminals target gun owners just the same those who choose to refrain from practicing their Second Amendment Right. The ironic part of this situation&nbsp;is we are actually on the same side of the issue, that is if your real intention is to stop criminals from obtaining firearms. Unfortunately I and many others in the community have a feeling there is a more sinister, ulterior motive behind this move. This is another attempt by the gun control crowd to restrict law abiding citizens from obtaining firearms. The only reasonable explanation as to why you would do such a thing, is if you wanted to incrementally move&nbsp;toward a national registry of all firearms. Those of us who are stewards of history know that registration always leads to confiscation. We all know that this is your ultimate goal, and slowly you are inching toward realizing your goal of disarming the American people. Don’t think we are blind to your plan. Trust me, we are well aware of what you’re trying to do. Just keep in mind we will not be led down the path of surrendering&nbsp;our Second Amendment Rights away FOR ANY REASON. A free society is secured when its citizens keep and bear arms. We will fight to make sure that right will not be infringed, no matter what!</p> <p>Your rationale doesn’t make sense. Criminals will always find a way to obtain firearms, regardless of what Facebook does with its groups. Even without Facebook’s gun groups, there will always be a way to easily obtain illegal items. History has shown this to be the case with every prohibition enacted. Make something illegal and see how fast that item&nbsp;is quickly and readily available on the black market. And often, for significantly less then what it cost before. This new move by facebook and your organization only makes it more difficult for LAW-ABIDING dealers and citizens to legally conduct lawful transactions with one another which is not the American way.</p> <h4 style="font-size: 125%; text-align: left;">Do you really think that Facebook Closes Gun Groups, Groups whose primary focus was to conduct lawful transactions between law-abiding citizens is going to stop gun violence in this country?</h4> <p>Are you so set in your liberal ways that you have become delusional to the point of actually believing that your leftist policy will even make a dent in gun violence in this country? Where are the studies and statistics about&nbsp;the number of&nbsp;guns bought on Facebook, legally or illegally, which have been used in a crime? Used to commit assault or battery on another person? Used in a murder?</p> <h5 style="font-size: 125%; text-align: left;">I would like&nbsp;to see those statistics. And see if what your organization and Facebook have done has actually done&nbsp;anything to decrease the frequency of these crimes.</h5> <p style="font-size: 100%; text-align: left;">I can almost guarantee that your decision to facebook closes gun groups will actually increase gun violence, because it is my belief that when law abiding citizens are legally armed, criminals know, and they are less likely to attack or target an individual that they think might possess a firearm.</p> <p style="font-size: 100%; text-align: left;">Hopefully Mrs. Watts, you will never have to face a situation where a firearm could have prevented a brutal attack on your or your family, and as a result of your unrealistic and misinformed bias against firearms, you become a victim of a crime that could have been prevented by lawfully carrying a concealed firearm.</p> <p style="font-size: 175%; text-align: center;"><strong>But Mrs. Watts, you will never face that situation, will you? Because like the hypocrite you are, you have armed&nbsp;bodyguards protecting you 24/7. Isn’t that right?</strong></p> <div id="attachment_15387" style="width: 510px" class="wp-caption aligncenter"><img class="wp-image-15387 size-large" src="http://i1.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/Moms-Demand-Has-armed-security.jpg?resize=500%2C330" alt="facebook-closes-gun-groups" srcset="http://i1.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/Moms-Demand-Has-armed-security.jpg?resize=500%2C330 500w, http://i1.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/Moms-Demand-Has-armed-security.jpg?resize=50%2C33 50w, http://i1.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/Moms-Demand-Has-armed-security.jpg?resize=200%2C132 200w, http://i1.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/Moms-Demand-Has-armed-security.jpg?resize=100%2C66 100w, http://i1.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/Moms-Demand-Has-armed-security.jpg?resize=150%2C99 150w, http://i1.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/Moms-Demand-Has-armed-security.jpg?w=560 560w" sizes="(max-width: 500px) 100vw, 500px" data-recalc-dims="1"><p class="wp-caption-text">Erika Soto Lamb, Communications Director for the Everytown for Gun Safety campaign, an effort of newly joined anti-gun groups Mayors Against Illegal Guns and Moms Demand Action, admitted in a tweet to conservative pundit Dana Loesch that the Moms Demand Action team has armed security guards.</p></div> <p>How can you go around telling&nbsp;law abiding American citizens that firearms are evil and bad, when they are around you everywhere you go? Do you think just because the gun is not carried or owned by you that makes it any better? That’s&nbsp;ludicrous! You should understand the importance of the Right to bear arms seeing as&nbsp;you require them for your daily safety. I’m sorry Mrs. Watts I forgot, you are part of the elite who think the rules shouldn’t apply to you, and because you have money, you can do whatever you please. You may think the world works that way but in reality, it doesn’t. Your fraud is being exposed right here and&nbsp;now, and your anti-American stance on gun control is disgusting.</p> <p style="font-size: 200%; text-align: center;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;"><strong>YOU SHOULD BE ASHAMED OF YOURSELF!</strong></span></p> <p>Let’s all keep in mind here that Chicago has some of the toughest firearm laws in the country, and yet that city has the highest murder rate in the country. Why? <strong>BECAUSE CRIMINALS DON’T FOLLOW THE LAW!</strong> The Obama Administration refuses to enforce existing laws so they can say gun violence is out of control and thereby have cause to enact policies that will lead to the confiscation of legally owned personal firearms.</p> <p>We are not stupid Mrs. Watts, we know you end game. But let’s just pretend for a minute that you don’t want our guns, what would be better alternatives than for the Facebook closes gun groups option?</p> <h6 style="font-size: 100%; text-align: left;">How about instead of Facebook Closes Gun Groups and forcing these&nbsp;gun transactions&nbsp;underground, don’t you think&nbsp;following these options may&nbsp;have been a better alternative? I do.</h6> <ul> <li style="font-size: 100%; text-align: left;">Creating an Educational Campaign to teach people how to buy and sell legally.</li> <li style="font-size: 100%; text-align: left;">Lobbying Facebook to help its administrators screen members better</li> <li style="font-size: 100%; text-align: left;">Lobbying Facebook to provide tools that would help identify under age users</li> <li style="font-size: 100%; text-align: left;">Launching a “see something say something” campaign in the groups to make members aware of potential red flags that they should look for before buying or selling a firearm to another member</li> <li style="font-size: 100%; text-align: left;">Give group members a quick and easy way to report a person to an administrator that raises red flags? or even Facebook if needed?</li> <li style="font-size: 100%; text-align: left;">Names of users matching local arrest records?</li> </ul> <p>I think that any one of these&nbsp;alternatives&nbsp;would have been a more effective approach&nbsp;than closing the&nbsp;groups IF YOUR TRUE intentions were to stop criminals from obtaining guns, don’t you? &nbsp;We are all adults here. We understand that as administrators and group members we have a responsibility to keep our communities safe, for ourselves and for the other members in the group. That is why we already self police and make sure to the best of our ability that everyone is following the law.</p> <p>I really hope you read this email, because you need to surround yourself with people who actually have real life solutions to the problems you are trying to solve. Instead, it seems like you are surrounded by your political left wing friends who know nothing about what actually goes on inside these groups, especially the fact that law enforcement was using them as a tool to stop criminals from purchasing firearms by monitoring them regularly. <strong>Congratulations!</strong> You have now made it easier for criminals to stay under the radar with the illegal gun trade and harder for law-abiding citizens and law-abiding dealers to&nbsp;conduct business.</p> <p>Realize this:&nbsp;<strong><em>Nothing you do will ever stop or deter gun violence in this country.</em></strong>&nbsp;The only thing that could deter a criminal from obtaining, carrying or selling a firearm, would be to impose strict minimum mandatory sentencing guidelines for criminals who are caught possessing or using a firearm. 20 years in prison would make a lot criminals think twice before carrying a firearm, and the ones who break the law and commit a crime with an illegally obtained firearm should be put in jail for a long time. Period. Other than that, good luck trying to combat a problem that doesn’t really exist in the first place.</p> <p style="font-size: 125%; text-align: left;"><strong>One more question – Why is it that ISIS is allowed to recruit members for global jihad on the same platform that now law-abiding gun buyers and sellers can no longer use?</strong> <span style="text-decoration: underline;">Which&nbsp;is the bigger threat?</span> ISIS? or two guys legally conducting a private firearms transaction of which 99.99% will never even see the sunlight other than at a local range. You need to really examine your reality.</p> <p>Thank you for making my years of investment in marketing and advertising dollars go right down the drain, and slow down my ability to make a living lawfully selling firearms on social media. Criminals will always find a way to get what they want. Your actions will only make it harder to detect illegal activity and prosecute it now.</p> <p style="font-size: 200%; text-align: center;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;">If you liked the letter, SHARE IT! Click Below</span><a href="https://www.facebook.com/sharer/sharer.php?u=http%3A//floridagunclassifieds.com/facebook-closes-gun-groups/" target="_blank"><br> </a></p> <p style="font-size: 200%; “Confiscate All Firearms”&nbsp;Before Leaving The White House.">First Lady Vocal Over Gun Control: Promises to “Confiscate All Firearms”&nbsp;Before Leaving The White House.</a></h3> <p class="meta dotted"><span class="dashicons-before user"><a href="http://floridagunclassifieds.com/author/matt-adika/" title="Posts by Matt Adika" rel="author">Matt Adika</a></span> <span class="dashicons-before <div class="entry-content"> <h1 class="cat_article_title">First Lady Vocal Over Gun Control: Promises to “Confiscate All Firearms”&nbsp;Before Leaving The White House.</h1> <p><img class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-14847" src="http://i1.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/Obama-First-Lady.jpg?resize=500%2C281" alt="obama-confiscate-firearms" srcset="http://i1.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/Obama-First-Lady.jpg?w=640 640w, http://i1.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/Obama-First-Lady.jpg?resize=50%2C28 50w, http://i1.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/Obama-First-Lady.jpg?resize=200%2C113 200w, http://i1.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/Obama-First-Lady.jpg?resize=500%2C281 500w, http://i1.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/Obama-First-Lady.jpg?resize=100%2C56 100w, http://i1.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/Obama-First-Lady.jpg?resize=150%2C84 150w" sizes="(max-width: 640px) 100vw, 640px" data-recalc-dims="1"></p> <div id="article_content" class="single_article_content"> <div></div> <div class="code-block code-block-3"> <h2 style="font-size: 130%;">First Lady Vocal Over Gun Control According to recent reports, Michelle recently decided to appear in Chicago to beg for more gun control. She stated that she and her husband both promise to “Confiscate all firarms” before they leave office in January 2017. Chicago was an interesting choice for the venue, given that they have both the strictest urban gun control laws, as well as the highest homicide rate in the nation. This topic is an interesting one because there is a lot of push back from law abiding citizens taunting Obama to “come and try and take my guns”.</h2> </div> <h3 style="font-size: 100%;">Just like her husband, The&nbsp;First Lady vocal over gun control decided to make herself the focal part of the story. When she spoke of Hadiya Pendleton, a&nbsp;teenage girl who performed at the Obama’s second Inauguration and was killed shortly after by gun-fired, Obama couldn’t help making the story about her own struggles.&nbsp;“Hadiya Pendleton was me and I was her,” Michelle told the audience, “But I got to grow and attend&nbsp;Princeton and Harvard Law School, I got to have a career and a family and the most blessed life I could ever imagine. And Hadiya, well we know that story. Just a week after she performed at my husband’s inauguration, she went to a park with some friends and got shot in the back.”</h3> <p>In addition to talking about herself, Michelle took the opportunity to push stricter gun control laws in Chicago. Despite the&nbsp;hard lefts showing a direct correlation between gun laws,&nbsp;shootings and murder, the agenda is nothing but more hypocrisy given that both she&nbsp;and her children have&nbsp;armed secret service agents 24/7 wherever they go.</p> <h4 style="font-size: 150%;">What do you think of&nbsp;The&nbsp;First Lady vocal over gun control?&nbsp;Let us know in the comments below and read our other article on <a href="http://floridagunclassifieds.com/gun-control-conspiracy/" target="_blank">The&nbsp;Gun Control Conspiracy</a>!</h4> <p>We think with the The First Lady vocal over gun control&nbsp;type talk from Michelle&nbsp;is not only dangerous, but irresponsible and wreckless. Michelle Obama is a smart woman. She knows how to read the data from various sources that shows whenever there are stricter gun laws and less private law abiding citizens carrying a concealed weapon, the higher the violent crime and murder rate becomes.</p> <p>If Mr. and Mrs Obama succeed in passing strict gun control measures in the USA before they leave office, it will directly impact the violent crime and murder rate to rise across the country. I believe this is a orchestrated event by the elite to destroy the fabric that holds this country together. If you know the statistics, and know how to interpret that data, then there is no other explanation other then malicious intent. We know when criminals know they might have to face an armed civilian, they are less likely to commit a violent crime because they know they&nbsp;might have to face an armed patriot.</p> <h5 style="font-size: 150%;">So what would our beautiful nation look like if the 2nd amendment was changed or removed? and our right to bear arms for protection of self, family and country&nbsp;no longer existed? What does the&nbsp;<span>First Lady vocal over gun control look like?</span></h5> <p style="font-size: 250%; text-align: center;">One Word:<em> <strong>Iraq</strong></em></p> <p>The reason why ISIS has become such a dominate force in the middle east is because the individual citizens did not have the right the bear arms to defend one another and there country, so like any creature or civilization without the means to defend itself, it either dies or gets taken over and destroyed. It could be a real possibility that in the near future we could look out our window and see black Islamic flags flying over every home, office building and even the White House.</p> <p><em>Sound impossible?</em> History shows us that if left unchecked, evil will continue to grow and spread like a cancer until it is eradicated by killing it. There are treatments that could shrink or stop the growth of the cancer, but until that cancer is killed or removed, it will never disappear by itself. Drastic action must be taken as quick as possible in order to stop the terrorists in their tracks. The First Lady Vocal over Gun Control only means the further deterioration of our beautiful country, we can only pray for someone like <a href="https://www.donaldjtrump.com/" target="_blank">Donald Trump</a> to win the election and shake up Washington.</p> <p><em>Written by:</em></p> <p><img class="wp-image-1892 size-medium alignleft" href="http://floridagunclassifieds.com/firearm-suppressor-sales/" title="Firearm Suppressor Sales Expected To Explode in 2016">Firearm Suppressor Sales Expected To Explode in 2016</a></h3> <p class="meta dotted"><span class="dashicons-before user"><a href="http://floridagunclassifieds.com/author/matt-adika/" title="Posts by Matt Adika" rel="author">Matt Adika</a></span> <span class="dashicons-before folderb"><a href="http://floridagunclassifieds.com/category/firearms-blog/" rel="category tag">Firearms Blog</a></span> <span class="dashicons-before clock"><span>January 21, 2016</span></span></p> <div class="entry-content"> <h1 class="pic-container dc-featured-image">Firearm Suppressor Sales Expected&nbsp;To Explode in 2016</h1> <p><img class="alignnone" src="http://i1.wp.com/14544-presscdn-0-64.pagely.netdna-cdn.com/wp-content/uploads/2012/12/gt51.jpg?resize=450%2C300" alt="firearm-suppressor-sales" data-recalc-dims="1"></p> <p>LAS VEGAS — SHOT SHOW 2016</p> <h2 class="pic-container dc-featured-image">Industry firearm professionals and gun organization officials are forecasting firearms suppressors or “silencers” as being the next hot item that firearm enthusiasts will be purchasing in&nbsp;2016 and continuing strong into 2017.</h2> <p>In this article we are going to discuss <strong>how to buy suppressor silencer in Florida</strong> and what new rule changes that were just introduced in the beginning of 2016 that is going to make how to buy suppressor silencer in Florida an easy, seamless process, which will drive up NFA sales making it the single largest growth category in the firearms industry.</p> <h2 style="font-size: 125%; text-align: left;">Matt Adika, President and Owner of this site Florida Gun Classifieds and the main contributor to this firearms blog, attended Shot Show in Las Vegas this year and had the privilege of speaking to <span>Josh Waldron, CEO of </span><a href="https://silencerco.com/" target="_blank">Silencer Co</a><span>.,</span> one of the countries largest distributor and manufacturer of suppressors silencers in the US. He gave us some insight on what we can expect this year and next due to the rule change announced early January 2016 removing the CLEO signature requirement from the Form 4.</h2> <p class="pic-container dc-featured-image">Josh Waldron, CEO of <a href="https://silencerco.com/" target="_blank">Silencer Co</a>., told Florida Gun Classifieds&nbsp;Tuesday at SHOT Show that it is much more difficult to get a suppressor than to get a firearm. “Suppressors are the most regulated consumer product, probably, in the United States,” said Waldron.</p> <div id="dc-word-up"> <p>Currently in order to obtain any NFA item, specifically a suppressor silencer in Florida, you must either:</p> <ol> <li>Obtain a signature from your Chief Law Enforcement Officer (Chief or Sheriff)</li> <li>Submit (2) copies of the Form 4 via a Class 03 firearms dealer (must be printed front and back of each page, so page 1 should be on the front of the paper, and if you flip the paper over page 2 should be on the back.</li> <li>Include two sets of fingerprint cards and two sets of passport photos.</li> <li>Include a $200 check/money order or now credit card payment to BATF to pay for the tax stamp.</li> <li>Wait for your $200 tax stamp to arrive in the mail from the ATF (currently about 6 months from time of submission). Once you receive the stamp, you can now go to your class 03 FFL dealer to pick up the suppressor silencer. &nbsp;ATF form 4473 must be completed and a NICS background check must be performed on the trustee that is picking up the suppressor silencer.</li> </ol> <p>OR</p> <ol> <li>Have a firearms trust with specific language that specifically discusses NFA items, how to handle these items in case of death or incapacitate, and the trust must be ratified to become an active legal document. A trust is treated as a “person” under US law just as a corporation acts as its own entity. In Florida a trust must have: <ol> <li><strong>Grantor</strong> – a person who created the trust and also acts as a trustee of the trust</li> <li><strong>Co-Trustee or Successor Trustee</strong> – a person who will carry out fiduciary duties in the event the Grantor becomes incapacitated or dies. Must be 21 years or older and pass a federal background check to make sure they are legally allowed to possess that NFA item.</li> <li><strong>Beneficiary</strong> – designated by the Grantor when creating the trust. The trust instructs the co-trustee or successor trustee on what to do with the assets inside the trust for the benefit of the beneficiary. *A beneficiary can be a minor as long as the trust specifically deals with what&nbsp;to do if the Grantor becomes incapacitated or dies while the beneficiary is still a minor.</li> <li><strong>Must be ratified</strong> under the laws of your particular state. In Florida each Trustee and Co-Trustee must have their signatures witnessed and verified by a notary public, as well as (2) witnesses who also verify the signer is present and signed the document.</li> <li><strong>Purchase your suppressor</strong> and Submit (2) copies of the Form 4, and (2) copies of your trust via a Class 03 firearms dealer (Form 4 must be printed front and back of each page, so page 1 should be on the front of the paper, and if you flip the paper over page 2 should be on the back.) <ol> <li>If you purchase a suppressor silencer and submit the form 4 before July 18th, 2016 you do not have to submit fingerprints or photographs of any of the trustees if the trust is purchasing the suppressor silencer.</li> <li>After July 18th, 2016 you must also include (2) copies of every trustee’s fingerprint cards and passport photos to be submitted with the form 4.</li> </ol> </li> <li><strong>Wait for your $200 tax stamp</strong> to arrive in the mail from the ATF (right now the wait is about 6 months). Once you receive the stamp, do your happy dance and head over to your class 03 FFL dealer to pick up the suppressor silencer. &nbsp;ATF form 4473 must be completed for the trustee picking up the suppressor silencer and a NICS background check must be approved before leaving with your new toy.</li> </ol> </li> </ol> <ul> <li>*NOTE: ATF is currently revamping their E-FORMS system, which currently only allows Form 1 to be completed online without having to mail any paper to the ATF. They introduced this new system at Shot Show 2016 and say once implemented, will remove much of the waiting time from applications. <ul> <li>Form 3, which is for class 03 dealers to transfer items to each other.</li> <li>Form 4, which is the application for an NFA item purchased from a Class 03 dealer. Once submitted, they will be automatically distributed to an ATF examiner for electronic processing and nothing has to be submitted through the mail.</li> </ul> </li> </ul> <h3 style="font-size: 100%; text-align: left;">When the rule change is implemented July 18th, 2016, you will now have to submit fingerprints and passport photos with every application, regardless of using a firearms trust. This adds a little bit of work to the process, but it sure beats trying to get your Chief law enforcement officer to sign off on your Form 4, an almost impossible task unless you know him personally.</h3> <p>If this process sounds complicated, having a knowledgeable, licensed FFL and SOT class 03 dealer to walk you through it&nbsp;will make the process smooth and seamless. <a href="http://floridagunclassifieds.com" target="_blank">Florida Gun Classifieds</a>&nbsp;specializes in Class 03 NFA items, give us a call or stop in and let us help you through the process.</p> <p><span>Josh Waldron, CEO of </span><a href="https://silencerco.com/" target="_blank">Silencer Co</a><span>., continued to tell Matt Adika president of Florida Gun Classifieds&nbsp;Tuesday at Shot Show that they think suppressors should be removed from the NFA classification.&nbsp;</span>“We support the Hearing Protection Act that was introduced on October 22nd, 2015 which is a piece of legislation that is aimed at removing suppressors / silencers from the NFA and instead having their transfer go through a traditional ATF form 4473 – the exact same way a person would purchase a standard rifle or pistol from a FFL dealer.”</p> </div> <p style="font-size: 175%; text-align: left;">What does this mean for you?</p> <ul> <li>No $200 tax stamp.</li> <li>No excessive wait times.</li> <li>No fingerprint cards, passport photos, or Chief Law Enforcement Officer signature.</li> <li>No NFA trusts, unless you want to be able to transfer ownership of the suppressor / silencer in case of death which can also be done by regular means such as a will.</li> </ul> <p>This proposed legislation would make purchasing a suppressor silencer a simple process, just like purchasing most firearms through your dealer.</p> <p>“Citizens should not be taxed for trying to protect their hearing while exercising their Second Amendment rights.” said Adika, president of Florida Gun Classifieds. “We support the Hearing Protection Act because it makes sense. Anyone who owns a suppressor silencer knows its not what Hollywood makes them out to be”. The Hearing Protection Act also includes a provision for all people who purchase a silencer between the time the bill is introduced until the day it passes, so should you purchase a silencer during that time, you will receive a $200 tax credit to cover the cost of any new silencer tax stamps you pay for.</p> <p>This bill is championed by Rep. Matt Salmon (R-AZ), its primary sponsor. Rep. Salmon hails from Arizona’s 5th District, and as a member of the Freedom Caucus is a great supporter of the Second Amendment and personal liberties. He is also a fellow owner of NFA products.</p> <div id="dc-word-up"> <h4 style="font-size: 125%; text-align: left;">So how does all this affect&nbsp;industry experts&nbsp;prediction that the suppressor silencer sales&nbsp;will explode in 2016 and 2017?</h4> <p>In 180 days, as a result of the Obama administration’s executive actions on National Firearms Act trusts, consumers will be able to purchase gun suppressors without needing the sign off of the chief law enforcement officer from the county they live in.&nbsp;Instead, FBI background checks as well as fingerprints and photo IDs will be required. This new rule will not only apply to purchases of gun suppressors but also fully automatic weapons, short-barreled rifles or a short-barreled shotguns.</p> <div id="outbrain_widget_0" class="OUTBRAIN" data-src="http://dailycaller.com/2016/01/19/silencer-industry-expected-to-expand-under-new-atf-rule/" data-widget-id="AR_2" data-ob-template="TheDailyCaller" data-ob-mark="true" data-browser="chrome" data-os="win32" data-dynload=""> <div class="ob-widget ob-strip-layout AR_2"> <div class="ob-widget-section ob-first"> <div class="ob-widget-header">“It’s still a lengthy process, but now we don’t have a problem where some sheriffs wouldn’t sign, because they are not pro second amendment. Some guys didn’t want the responsibility so they refused to sign,” Waldron said. “So that was a big reason why people used trusts. It was because you didn’t need to get that signature, but now with trusts you do have to do fingerprints and photo IDs. So it was kind of a give-and-take from the industry.”</div> </div> </div> </div> <p>In preparation for the rule change Waldron’s Silencer Co. is pushing out a new campaign to explain to the public why law gun owners would use silencers, a concept that tends to be unknown to most people outside the gun industry.</p> <p>“The fight the noise campaign is a grassroots effort to change the way people really view silencers or suppressors. It’s an education campaign &nbsp;just as much as its an advocacy&nbsp;campaign,” said Waldron. “Basically we want to have a paradigm shift, so that when someone sees a suppressor they think of hearing protection and not of what Hollywood wants to portray, because that’s not what it really is.”</p> <p>“It’s hearing protection. And the biggest thing is, if you think about it, if you’re wearing your hearing protection, whether your ear muffs or ear plugs, you can’t hear your surroundings when you’re hunting so hunters don’t use them when they’re hunting. So it’s really a hearing loss problem that that all hunters [come across],” Waldron noted, adding that his own dog went deaf.</p> <p>“You train these dogs to go out with you and they’re right next to you and they’re right by your side and you’re constantly shooting and nobody thinks about the dog’s hearing. You&nbsp;spend all that time and effort to train these dogs and then they go deaf. They’re &nbsp;basically useless for hunting,” he said.</p> <p>Waldron said the suppressor issue has not received any political pushback and 30 pro-suppressor bills passed different state legislatures in the past four years. He views gun suppressors as a bipartisan safety product as opposed to what an assassin may use to take out a target.</p> <p>“Silencers are not what people think they are. They’re not as quiet as people think they are, and there just hasn’t been a problem on the books, so there just hasn’t been a reason, because they are [going to be] easier to buy,” Waldron explained.</p> <p>“You just have to do a background check. We’re&nbsp;not all of a sudden going to have spike or a rash of violent crimes committed with silencers, because we haven’t had that in the past,” he added.</p> </div> <p>&nbsp;</p> <div tag-concealed-carry-firearm tag-cwp tag-good-guns-with-guns tag-how-to-stop-mass-shootings tag-mass-shooting tag-stopping-mass-shootings" id="post-13638"> <div class="shadowblock"> <div class="dashicons-before comment-bubble"><a href="http://floridagunclassifieds.com/guns-stopped-mass-shootings/#respond" class="bubble cp-fixed-color">0</a></div> <h3 class="loop"><a href="http://floridagunclassifieds.com/guns-stopped-mass-shootings/" title="Guns Stopped Mass Shootings 12 Times by Good Guys With Guns">Guns Stopped Mass Shootings 12 Times by Good Guys With Guns</a></h3> <p class="meta dotted"><span class="dashicons-before user"><a href="http://floridagunclassifieds.com/author/matt-adika/" title="Posts by Matt Adika" rel="author">Matt Adika</a></span> <span class="dashicons-before folderb"><a href="http://floridagunclassifieds.com/category/firearms-blog/" rel="category tag">Firearms Blog</a></span> <span class="dashicons-before clock"><span>December 18, 2015</span></span></p> <div class="entry-content"> <img width="150" height="138" src="http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/Mag-Cover-12-times-good-guys-stopped-mass-shootings.jpg?fit=150%2C138" class="attachment-blog-thumbnail size-blog-thumbnail wp-post-image" alt="Guns Stopped Mass Shootings" srcset="http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/Mag-Cover-12-times-good-guys-stopped-mass-shootings.jpg?w=522 522w, http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/Mag-Cover-12-times-good-guys-stopped-mass-shootings.jpg?resize=50%2C46 50w, http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/Mag-Cover-12-times-good-guys-stopped-mass-shootings.jpg?resize=163%2C150 163w, http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/Mag-Cover-12-times-good-guys-stopped-mass-shootings.jpg?resize=500%2C459 500w, http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/Mag-Cover-12-times-good-guys-stopped-mass-shootings.jpg?resize=100%2C92 100w, http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/Mag-Cover-12-times-good-guys-stopped-mass-shootings.jpg?resize=150%2C138 150w" sizes="(max-width: 150px) 100vw, 150px"> <h2 style="font-size: 100%; text-align: center;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;">Guns Stopped Mass Shootings 12 Times by Good Guys With Guns.</span></h2> <p style="font-size: 100%; text-align: center;">Hopefully as you read this article, you will begin to see a pattern start to emerge that <strong>Guns Stopped Mass Shootings</strong> from becoming a lot worse these 12 times.&nbsp;We all want to find the “<span style="text-decoration: underline;">Magic Bullet</span>” to prevent these mass shootings from happening in the first place. Stricter gun laws, banning firearms, harsher penalties for committing crimes and carrying a firearm without the proper credentials are all ideas behind how to stop these mass shootings from ever occurring, but lets be realistic; Regardless of what legislation we pass, there might not be a way to prevent these tragedies from occurring, but we can definitely lower the number of causalities by doing one simple thing:</p> <h3 style="font-size: 150%; text-align: center;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;"><strong>Encouraging civilians to legally carry a firearm.</strong></span></h3> <p>If we look at the facts and statistics and make decisions based on real data, without all the bias media lies, we can see that when there are good guys with concealed weapons who have the correct training to use that firearm are present when a mass shooting occurs, there are less casualties because that person had the ability to take heroic action and protect himself and his fellow men and women. <strong>Here are the top 12 times good guys with guns stopped mass shootings from becoming much much worse.</strong> Ask you self: if we encouraged every American to carry a concealed weapon. “<span style="text-decoration: underline;">How many lives could we save if and when another shooting like San Bernardino took place?</span>”</p> <p style="font-size: 100%; text-align: left; padding-left: 30px;"><strong>1. Pearl High School</strong></p> <p><img class="aligncenter wp-image-13639 size-large" src="http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/Mag-Cover-12-times-good-guys-stopped-mass-shootings.jpg?resize=500%2C459" alt="Guns Stopped Mass Shootings" srcset="http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/Mag-Cover-12-times-good-guys-stopped-mass-shootings.jpg?resize=500%2C459 500w, http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/Mag-Cover-12-times-good-guys-stopped-mass-shootings.jpg?resize=50%2C46 50w, http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/Mag-Cover-12-times-good-guys-stopped-mass-shootings.jpg?resize=163%2C150 163w, http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/Mag-Cover-12-times-good-guys-stopped-mass-shootings.jpg?resize=100%2C92 100w, http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/Mag-Cover-12-times-good-guys-stopped-mass-shootings.jpg?resize=150%2C138 150w, http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/Mag-Cover-12-times-good-guys-stopped-mass-shootings.jpg?w=522 522w" sizes="(max-width: 500px) 100vw, 500px" data-recalc-dims="1"></p> <p><strong>Oct. 1, 1997</strong><br> Luke Woodham fatally stabbed his mother at home before opening fire at his high school,&nbsp;killing two students and injuring seven others. The attack <a href="http://frontpagemag.com/2012/dgreenfield/how-an-assistant-principal-with-a-gun-stopped-a-school-shooter/" target="_blank">was stopped</a> when Assistant Principal Joel Myrick retrieved his .45 caliber handgun from his truck and confronted Woodham, detaining him until authorities could arrive. This is a case were&nbsp;Guns Stopped Mass Shootings from becoming worse.</p> <p>Myrick’s action stopped Woodham from going across the street to the middle school as he had planned.</p> <p style="font-size: 100%; text-align: left;"><strong>2. Parker Middle School</strong></p> <p><img class="aligncenter wp-image-7806 size-full" src="http://i0.wp.com/1y7vgdz53a11xyb91s53s6d6.wpengine.netdna-cdn.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/06/0623A4.jpg?resize=500%2C234" alt="Guns Stopped Mass Shootings" data-recalc-dims="1"></p> <p><strong>April 24, 1998</strong><br> A 14-year-old student&nbsp;showed up to his middle school dance carrying a .25-caliber pistol. He opened fire inside the dance, killing one teacher and wounding another as well as two students.&nbsp;The rampage&nbsp;ended when James Strand, owner of the banquet hall the dance was happening in, grabbed his personal shotgun and confronted the 14-year-old killer. Strand&nbsp;held the teen at gunpoint&nbsp;for 11 minutes before finally getting him to drop the weapon and lie on the ground and searching him for additional weapons. Without this law abiding citizen, the&nbsp;Guns Stopped Mass Shootings wouldn’t have applied here.</p> <p style="font-size: 125%; text-align: left;"><strong>3. Appalachian School of Law</strong></p> <p><img class="aligncenter wp-image-13649 size-large" src="http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/3-mass-shootings.jpg?resize=500%2C242" alt="Guns Stopped Mass Shootings" srcset="http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/3-mass-shootings.jpg?resize=500%2C242 500w, http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/3-mass-shootings.jpg?resize=50%2C24 50w, http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/3-mass-shootings.jpg?resize=200%2C97 200w, http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/3-mass-shootings.jpg?resize=100%2C48 100w, http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/3-mass-shootings.jpg?resize=150%2C72 150w, http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/3-mass-shootings.jpg?w=625 625w" sizes="(max-width: 500px) 100vw, 500px" data-recalc-dims="1"></p> <p><strong>Jan. 16, 2002</strong><br> A&nbsp;43-year-old former student armed with a .380 handgun&nbsp;killed Dean&nbsp;Anthony Sutin and&nbsp;Professor Thomas Blackwell with point blank shots and went on to kill fellow student Angela Dales as well as wounding three others before being confronted at gunpoint by&nbsp;law students Tracy Bridges, a county sheriff’s deputy, and Mikael Gross, a police officer, after retrieving their personal handguns from their vehicles. The gunman was then apprehended by other students.</p> <p>Gross and Bridges lost valuable response time&nbsp;accessing their handguns because of the law school’s standing as a gun-free zone.&nbsp;Guns Stopped Mass Shootings in the past, why would we encourage gun free zones where we are sitting ducks?</p> <p style="font-size: 125%; text-align: left; padding-left: 30px;"><strong>4. New Life Church</strong></p> <p><img class="aligncenter wp-image-13640 size-large" src="http://i1.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/4new-church-shooting.jpg?resize=500%2C325" alt="Guns Stopped Mass Shootings" srcset="http://i1.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/4new-church-shooting.jpg?resize=500%2C325 500w, http://i1.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/4new-church-shooting.jpg?resize=50%2C33 50w, http://i1.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/4new-church-shooting.jpg?resize=200%2C130 200w, http://i1.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/4new-church-shooting.jpg?resize=100%2C65 100w, http://i1.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/4new-church-shooting.jpg?resize=150%2C98 150w, http://i1.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/4new-church-shooting.jpg?w=600 600w" sizes="(max-width: 500px) 100vw, 500px" data-recalc-dims="1"></p> <p><strong>Dec. 9, 2007</strong><br> 2 parishioners were killed and 3 wounded when a gunman toting a Bushmaster AR-15 opened fire at New Hope Church. Hearing the rifle fire, &nbsp;Jeanne Assam grabbed her personal concealed carry firearm and confronted the gunman from a distance of 20 yards. Guns Stopped Mass Shootings According to <a href="http://www.5280.com/magazine/2012/12/jeanne-assam-still-waiting" target="_blank">this article in 5280 magazine</a>:</p> <blockquote><p>She fires five quick shots. Murray falls backward. Assam moves to the middle of the corridor and rushes forward. She’s a few dozen feet from Murray now, exposed in the middle of the hallway. “Drop your weapon, or I will kill you!” she yells. Murray sits up to face her. He’s still holding the rifle. Boom-boom-boom. Bullets rip past her and pepper a wall. While Murray shoots, Assam fires three times.</p> <p>Through the haze of gun smoke, Assam sees the man struggling on the floor. He props his head against a wall. Her weapon is up, trained on the man. She sees his hands moving near his shoulder. He’s trying to pull the pin on a grenade. He’s going to kill everyone around here, Assam thinks. She instinctively steps back and fires two more shots.</p></blockquote> <p style="font-size: 125%; text-align: left; padding-left: 30px;"><strong>5. New York Mills AT&amp;T Store</strong></p> <p><img class="aligncenter wp-image-13641 size-large" src="http://i1.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/5new-york-mills-att-shooting.jpg?resize=500%2C298" alt="Guns Stopped Mass Shootings new-york-mass-shooting-legal" srcset="http://i1.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/5new-york-mills-att-shooting.jpg?resize=500%2C298 500w, http://i1.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/5new-york-mills-att-shooting.jpg?resize=50%2C30 50w, http://i1.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/5new-york-mills-att-shooting.jpg?resize=200%2C119 200w, http://i1.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/5new-york-mills-att-shooting.jpg?resize=100%2C60 100w, http://i1.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/5new-york-mills-att-shooting.jpg?resize=150%2C90 150w, http://i1.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/5new-york-mills-att-shooting.jpg?w=650 650w" sizes="(max-width: 500px) 100vw, 500px" data-recalc-dims="1"></p> <p><strong>May 27, 2010</strong><br> A 79-year-old man entered an AT&amp;T store in New York Mills, New York carrying a .357 magnum revolver in his hand and a list of employees he planned to kill in his pocket. Hearing the hand cannon go off, Donald J. Moore drew his own personal weapon and Guns Stopped Mass Shootings here and killed the gunman before he could complete his plan. One employee was wounded in the shooting.</p> <p style="font-size: 125%; text-align: left; padding-left: 30px;"><strong>6. Sullivan Central High School</strong></p> <p><img class="aligncenter wp-image-13642 size-full" src="http://i1.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/6-sullivan-central-high-school-mass-shooting.jpg?resize=300%2C243" alt="Guns Stopped Mass Shootings in high school" srcset="http://i1.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/6-sullivan-central-high-school-mass-shooting.jpg?w=300 300w, http://i1.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/6-sullivan-central-high-school-mass-shooting.jpg?resize=50%2C41 50w, http://i1.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/6-sullivan-central-high-school-mass-shooting.jpg?resize=185%2C150 185w, http://i1.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/6-sullivan-central-high-school-mass-shooting.jpg?resize=100%2C81 100w, http://i1.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/6-sullivan-central-high-school-mass-shooting.jpg?resize=150%2C122 150w" sizes="(max-width: 300px) 100vw, 300px" data-recalc-dims="1"></p> <p><strong>August 30, 2010</strong><br> When a 62-year-old man armed with two handguns forced his way into Sullivan Central High School in Tennessee, he was immediately engaged by School Resource Officer Carolyn Gudger. Gudger put her body between the gunman and a student and started what would turn out to be a more than 10 minute gun-to-gun encounter. Gudger used the time to slowly move the man to a less crowded part of the school. When other officers arrived on the scene, a brief gun battle erupted ending with the gunman mortally wounded.&nbsp;Guns Stopped Mass Shootings.</p> <p style="font-size: 125%; text-align: left; padding-left: 30px;"><strong>7. Freewill Baptist Church</strong></p> <p><img class="aligncenter wp-image-13643 size-large" src="http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/7-free-will-baptist-church-shooting.jpg?resize=500%2C263" alt="Guns Stopped Mass Shootings at free will baptist church" srcset="http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/7-free-will-baptist-church-shooting.jpg?resize=500%2C263 500w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/7-free-will-baptist-church-shooting.jpg?resize=50%2C26 50w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/7-free-will-baptist-church-shooting.jpg?resize=200%2C105 200w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/7-free-will-baptist-church-shooting.jpg?resize=100%2C53 100w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/7-free-will-baptist-church-shooting.jpg?resize=150%2C79 150w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/7-free-will-baptist-church-shooting.jpg?w=640 640w" sizes="(max-width: 500px) 100vw, 500px" data-recalc-dims="1"></p> <p><strong>March 25, 2012</strong><br> Aaron Guyton was inside the recreation building of his grandfather’s church when he saw Jessie Gates, a member of the congregation, <a href="http://www.goupstate.com/article/20120325/ARTICLES/120329781/1112" target="_blank">pulling a shotgun from his vehicle</a>. Guyton leapt into action, locking the doors to the church where services were going on. Gates kicked in the door and pointed the shotgun at Rev. Henry Guyton and several parishioners. Drawing his concealed handgun, the younger Guyton held Gates at gunpoint while two members of the church took him to the ground. Guns Stopped Mass Shootings here and Rev. Guyton then took the shotgun from his hand.</p> <p style="font-size: 125%; text-align: left; padding-left: 30px;"><strong>8. Clackamas Town Center Mall</strong></p> <div id="attachment_13644" style="width: 510px" class="wp-caption aligncenter"><img class="wp-image-13644 size-large" src="http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/8-clackamas-shooting.jpg?resize=500%2C263" alt="Guns Stopped Mass Shootings" srcset="http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/8-clackamas-shooting.jpg?resize=500%2C263 500w, http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/8-clackamas-shooting.jpg?resize=50%2C26 50w, http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/8-clackamas-shooting.jpg?resize=200%2C105 200w, http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/8-clackamas-shooting.jpg?resize=100%2C53 100w, http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/8-clackamas-shooting.jpg?resize=150%2C79 150w, http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/8-clackamas-shooting.jpg?w=640 640w" sizes="(max-width: 500px) 100vw, 500px" data-recalc-dims="1"><p class="wp-caption-text">Police and medics work the scene of a multiple shooting at Clackamas Town Center Mall in Clackamas, Ore., Tuesday Dec. 11, 2012. A gunman is dead after opening fire in the Portland, Ore., area shopping mall Tuesday, killing two people and wounding another, sheriff’s deputies said. (AP Photo/Greg Wahl-Stephens)</p></div> <p><strong>Dec. 11, 2012</strong><br> Two people were killed and a third was seriously wounded at Clackamas Town Center near Portland, Oregon when a rifle-toting gunman&nbsp;opened fire in in the busy food court. Nick Meli, a shopper in the mall, drew a personally owned firearm on the gunman, who immediately&nbsp;retreated to a service corridor and killed himself. Meli did not fire his weapon for fear of striking bystanders yet authorities say his actions caused the gunman to cease his attack and end his own life.</p> <p style="font-size: 125%; text-align: left; padding-left: 30px;"><strong>9. Mystic Strip Club</strong></p> <p><img class="aligncenter wp-image-13645 size-large" src="http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/9mystic-strip-club-shooting.jpg?resize=500%2C263" alt="Guns Stopped Mass Shootings at strip club" srcset="http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/9mystic-strip-club-shooting.jpg?resize=500%2C263 500w, http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/9mystic-strip-club-shooting.jpg?resize=50%2C26 50w, http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/9mystic-strip-club-shooting.jpg?resize=200%2C105 200w, http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/9mystic-strip-club-shooting.jpg?resize=100%2C53 100w, http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/9mystic-strip-club-shooting.jpg?resize=150%2C79 150w, http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/9mystic-strip-club-shooting.jpg?w=640 640w" sizes="(max-width: 500px) 100vw, 500px" data-recalc-dims="1"></p> <p><strong>January 11, 2014</strong><br> After being refused entry to the strip club for belligerent behavior and racist comments earlir in the night,&nbsp;Thomas Elliott Hjelmeland returned carrying a handgun and wearing a Halloween mask. As soon as he entered the club, Hjelmeland opened fire, striking bouncer Brian Rizzo, a patron, and a waitress.&nbsp;Another bouncer, Jonathan Baer drew his concealed handgun and shot Hjelmeland, killing him.</p> <p>Following the attack Baer posted to Facebook: “Its a fact that&nbsp;Guns Stopped Mass Shootings time and time again. I did what I felt was right to stop the shooter…I carry every day, and will continue to, and will so with the hope that I will NEVER have to pull it out again.”</p> <p style="font-size: 125%; text-align: left; padding-left: 30px;"><strong>10. Austin, Texas Construction Site</strong></p> <p><img class="aligncenter wp-image-13646 size-large" src="http://i1.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/10-austin-texas-shooting.jpg?resize=500%2C263" alt="Guns Stopped Mass Shootings at construction site" srcset="http://i1.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/10-austin-texas-shooting.jpg?resize=500%2C263 500w, http://i1.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/10-austin-texas-shooting.jpg?resize=50%2C26 50w, http://i1.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/10-austin-texas-shooting.jpg?resize=200%2C105 200w, http://i1.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/10-austin-texas-shooting.jpg?resize=100%2C53 100w, http://i1.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/10-austin-texas-shooting.jpg?resize=150%2C79 150w, http://i1.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/10-austin-texas-shooting.jpg?w=640 640w" sizes="(max-width: 500px) 100vw, 500px" data-recalc-dims="1"></p> <p><strong>April 30, 2014</strong><br> An irate former employee came to a construction site and <a href="http://kxan.com/2014/04/30/2-hurt-in-shooting-near-downtown/" target="_blank">opened fire on his co-workers</a>. The site’s foreman, a Concealed Handgun License holder, drew his firearm and opened fire. Both men were wounded in the exchange of gunfire but the foreman’s actions ended the attack and no one else was wounded.</p> <p style="font-size: 125%; text-align: left; padding-left: 30px;"><strong>11. Cache Valley Hospital</strong></p> <p><img class="aligncenter wp-image-13647 size-full" src="http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/11-cache-hospital-shooting.jpg?resize=488%2C414" alt="Guns Stopped Mass Shootings at hospital" srcset="http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/11-cache-hospital-shooting.jpg?w=488 488w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/11-cache-hospital-shooting.jpg?resize=50%2C42 50w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/11-cache-hospital-shooting.jpg?resize=177%2C150 177w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/11-cache-hospital-shooting.jpg?resize=100%2C85 100w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/11-cache-hospital-shooting.jpg?resize=150%2C127 150w" sizes="(max-width: 488px) 100vw, 488px" data-recalc-dims="1"></p> <p><strong>May 16, 2014</strong><br> Armed with two handguns, a man entered the <a href="http://www.sltrib.com/sltrib/news/58238365-78/burr-emergency-attorney-report.html.csp" target="_blank">Cache Valley Hospital </a>emergency room and began making demands. After demanding to see a doctor, he racked the slide on one of his handguns and told hospital employees “someone is going to die today”. While a security guard tried to keep the gunman’s focus on him, two corrections officers who happened to be at the hospital on an unrelated matter engaged from another direction and prove the fact that Guns Stopped Mass Shootings. The gunman was shot three times and no other people were harmed.</p> <p style="font-size: 125%; text-align: left; padding-left: 30px;"><strong>12. Mercy Fitzgerald Hospital</strong></p> <p><img class="aligncenter wp-image-13648 size-large" src="http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/11-cache-shooting.jpg?resize=381%2C500" alt="Guns Stopped Mass Shootings" srcset="http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/11-cache-shooting.jpg?resize=381%2C500 381w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/11-cache-shooting.jpg?resize=38%2C50 38w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/11-cache-shooting.jpg?resize=114%2C150 114w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/11-cache-shooting.jpg?resize=76%2C100 76w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/11-cache-shooting.jpg?w=634 634w" sizes="(max-width: 381px) 100vw, 381px" data-recalc-dims="1"></p> <p><strong>July 25, 2014</strong><br> A patient at a psychiatric clinic killed his case worker at point blank range and then turned his gun on his doctor, Lee Silverman, striking him several times. Before the gunman could leave the office and continue his rampage, Dr. Silverman drew his own concealed handgun and pumped three rounds into&nbsp;the gunman’s torso, mortally wounding him. Police and hospital staff hail Dr. Silverman as a hero and credit him with saving dozens of lives.</p> <h4 style="text-align: center;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;"><strong>So what do these Mass Shootings show us about how&nbsp;Guns Stopped Mass Shootings?</strong></span></h4> <p>We can see that responsible gun ownership by law abiding citizens prevents zero threat, and can can definitively say that&nbsp;<strong>guns stopped mass shootings these 12 times</strong>. We need to understand in this country that the threat is here and is not going anywhere anytime soon. Instead of trying to <span style="text-decoration: underline;"><strong>BAN ALL GUNS</strong></span>, we should encourage more law abiding citizens to <span style="text-decoration: underline;"><strong>CARRY MORE GUNS</strong>.</span></p> <p style="font-size: 125%; text-align: center;"><strong><em>The only way to stop a bad guy with a gun is&nbsp;with&nbsp;a good guy with a gun.</em></strong></p> <p style="text-align: center;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;"><strong>Based on all this overwhelming evidence, why would be want to ban legal firearms?</strong></span></p> <p>Political pressure and leftist thinkers believe if we ban all guns, violent crime will decrease. Just remember: <strong><span style="text-decoration: underline;">CRIMINALS DO NOT FOLLOW LAWS</span>.</strong> So regardless of what anti-gun legislation is pushed through congress, it will do absolutely nothing to stop mass shootings, and based on this article, actually cause more deaths because there will be no good guys with guns to stop the mass shooting before the police have time to respond. Its time to stop listening to the leftist propaganda and look at the facts! <span style="text-decoration: underline;"><strong>GOOD GUYS WITH GUNS STOPPED MASS SHOOTINGS 12 Times!</strong></span> We need this to happen in every mass shooting every time. This is the only way to make our communities safe, arm and train every&nbsp;citizen and our communities will be safer as a result.</p> <p>Thank you to: Hunter Roosevelt for the great article</p> <p>Read more: <a href="http://controversialtimes.com/issues/constitutional-rights/12-times-mass-shootings-were-stopped-by-good-guys-with-guns/#ixzz3ueF4skJ8" target="_blank">Good Guns With Guns Stopping Mass Shootings</a>, best concealed carry gun, concealed carry, concealed carry firearm, cwp, Firearms Blog, good guns with guns, how to stop mass shootings, mass shooting, stopping mass 2015</span></span></p> <div class="entry-content"> <img width="150" height="94" src="http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/11/bostonbomb.jpg?fit=150%2C94" http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/11/bostonbomb.jpg?resize=150%2C94 150w" sizes="(max-width: 150px) 100vw, 150px"> <h2 class="title" style="text-align: center;">Ten Ways To Avoid Being Killed During A Terrorist Attack</h2> <div class="entry"> <p><img class="wp-image-146314" src="http://i2.wp.com/cdn.bearingarms.com/uploads/2015/11/800px-2013_Boston_Marathon_aftermath_people1-300x188.jpg?resize=500%2C313" alt="How to stay alive during a terrorist attack" width="500" height="313"></p> <p>&nbsp;</p> </div> <p>In light of Friday’s terrorist attacks, it seems only a matter of time before similar incidents occur in the U.S. The question many people are asking is “What would I do if suddenly in a situation like Paris?” &nbsp;To help answer that question, Florida Gun Classifieds has a created a list of ten things you can do to avoid&nbsp;becoming a casualty in the “War on Terror.”</p> <ol> <li><strong>Realize it WILL happen here –</strong> This isn’t a paranoid statement: it is a simple unpleasant fact based upon intelligence gathering efforts, expert opinion, and common sense. At some point, it is likely there will be a coordinated, Paris-type attack in the U.S. on schools, shopping malls, sporting events, or other mass-gathering areas. And, don’t think it would happen only in New York, Chicago or Los Angeles because what would be better to create fear (the ultimate goal of terrorist action) than by killing dozens or hundreds of people at a school in rural Mississippi or a shopping mall in Montana?</li> <li><strong>Always carry a concealed firearm where legal –</strong> Carrying a firearm is a lifestyle habit, not something you should do only occasionally or when you feel it is likely there will be trouble. Odds are, you won’t correctly guess the date, time and place of life-threatening violence. <strong><em>A concealed firearm in the hands of a responsible and trained individual is statistically one of the best tools available to stop mass killings.</em></strong></li> <li><strong>Improvised weapons are within reach –</strong> If you cannot or choose not to carry a firearm, there are always effective weapons within your immediate area so learn to use them. Whenever unarmed in a public area, make it a habit (or game) to choose three nearby items that would make a good weapon if things turn dire.</li> <li><strong>Know where exits are located –</strong> Many people die during all types of emergencies because they don’t know where exits are located.&nbsp; This should be the first thing you do, above all else, whenever situated in a public place.</li> <li><strong>Act decisively –</strong> The “immediate action drill” during an attack is either fight or flee. Don’t mill around, waiting for instruction or to gain a better idea of what is happening. Flee the area when you have an opportunity or instantly attack a threat if one presents itself. The old chestnut is still true: “To Ponder is to Perish.”</li> <li><strong>Be alert to people and unusual circumstances –</strong> Most folks wouldn’t see a large pink gorilla wandering down the hallway and certainly won’t see a suspicious individual fiddling with wires under a long trench coat on a hot day. You don’t have to glare at every passerby but simply maintain a loose focus for unusual patterns of activity within your surroundings. This is also known as “Maintaining Condition Yellow.”</li> <li><strong>“If you see something, say something.” –</strong> Cops everywhere have stories of witnesses who said after a crime, ‘I wasn’t sure what was going on and I didn’t want to make a big deal out of it.’&nbsp; If you see people or objects that look suspicious, notify the authorities immediately. There is no punishment for being mistaken but there are huge consequences to being correct but not sharing the information.</li> <li><strong>There is one more bomb/attack/assailant –</strong> Experience has shown that attackers are increasingly planning not only their initially assault, but follow-up actions such as secondary or even tertiary explosives and attackers. Such actions not only increase the “shock and awe” of the incident but cause additional carnage and damage the emergency response system.</li> <li><strong>Have a basic understanding of trauma medical care –</strong> in the aftermath of a bombing or shooting incident, many people will be bleeding to death and you have two or three minutes to save lives.&nbsp; This means you need to understand mass-casualty triage principals and some basic tactical combat casualty care (TCCC) techniques. Be ready to provide aid such as tourniquets, spinal immobilization and safe patient evacuation from threatening circumstances.</li> <li><strong>Trust your intuition –</strong> If something ‘feels’ dangerous or simply makes you uneasy, trust your inner voices. This inner dialog might be wrong, but then again, you may have subconsciously picked up subtle environmental clues that you “can’t quite put your finger on,” but are real nonetheless. At the very least, move to a safer position or relocate to where you can more easily escape a potential kill zone.</li> </ol> <p>It is not hyperbole to state that we are all now terrorism responder’s because the avowed goal of Daesh and other such groups is to bring death and destruction to Mainstreet U.S.A. However, with planning and preparation individual citizens can sometimes prevent, often shorten and effectively respond to mass killing incidents.</p> <p>The world is changing quickly, and you need to adapt to stay alive.&nbsp;Would you rather be prepared, armed and ready to take out any threat? Or be that victim that is just another number added to the body count on the nightly news? Ask yourself: <strong>Do I know how to stay alive during a terrorist attack?</strong> Am I ready to neutralize any threat that happens to present itself at anytime? Daytime, nighttime, on the bus, in a mall, at a restaurant, walking the dog, driving to work, picking up the kids, cashing your check. Can I protect not only myself but the people around&nbsp;me at any given moment in time?</p> <p>It is now our civil duty as Americans to be able to defend not only ourselves, but one another. In a time that will go down in history as the one of the most divisive times in American history, when our own president seeks to divide his people and pitted neighbor against neighbor, brother against sister, black against white, citizens against police, maybe this is God’s way of bringing Americans together once again for a higher purpose: To protect innocent lives against radical Islamic trash who seek to destroy our way of life. Remember, the enemy is unknown, he is not wearing any uniform, and cannot be distinguished from you or I. They are trained to blend in with us, live among us, eat, sleep, walk and shop with us. Essentially, they are us. The only thing that separates them from us is their ideology. They want us dead and we want to stay alive.</p> <p>Remember&nbsp;these three words: <em><strong>ANYWHERE, ANYTIME, ANYONE</strong></em>. You must practice <em><strong>situational awareness. </strong></em>It&nbsp;has to be your new way of life. Knowing everything that is happening around you at all times, and if something is out of place or seems like it doesn’t belong, you can’t just brush it off like we all used to on a daily basis. <em><strong>YOU MUST BE PREPARED TO ACT AT THE DROP OF A DIME AND TRAIN TO KILL THESE SCUMBAGS QUICKLY AND EFFECTIVELY</strong></em>. Referred to as <em><strong>Operation Kratos</strong></em>, Shooting an active target once is insufficient. You must train to NEUTRALIZE any threat by shooting the target&nbsp;multiple times, aiming directly for the <strong>BRAIN STEM.</strong> You must assume they are planning to detonate an explosive device AKA&nbsp;the suicide vest every time, and you must eliminate their ability to detonate their device by severing their spinal cord so they loose the ability to press that button and detonate their suicide vest. Suicide bombers are likely to detonate their devices as soon as they realize&nbsp;they had been identified. Tactics must ensure <strong><em>immediate incapacitation</em></strong> to give the bomber no opportunity to detonate the bomb. These tactics were developed by London’s Metropolitan Police Service for dealing with suspected suicide bombers, and teaches firing multiple shots into the head without warning, specifically&nbsp;aiming for the BRAIN STEM which is at the base of the head, connecting the head to the spine. The tactics were developed shortly after the September 11th , 2001 attacks, based in part on consultation with Israeli and Sri Lankan law enforcement agencies on how to deal with suicide bombers.</p> <p>As soon as a threat is identified, there is no time for hesitation, not even a second. Draw your firearm, and unload every round in your magazine directly at the base of the head of the terrorist. Make sure you have extra magazines because most attacks are not carried out by a single individual. Multiple attackers is a real and likely threat.</p> <p>After eliminating the first threat, quickly reload your firearm and scan the area for additional threats. Look for the person or people that are not running away from the shooting, but coming toward you or any area where there are a lot of people all in one spot. Anyone that is watching what is unfolding instead of running away could be&nbsp;that second&nbsp;possible threat. Aim your&nbsp;firearm directly at their brain stem and start giving verbal commands to show&nbsp;and&nbsp;raise their hands above their head. If they do not respond, this is a situation where you must assess the threat quickly and correctly to determine whether or not to engage.</p> <p>Ask yourself:</p> <ol> <li>what is the demeanor of the supposed target? <ol> <li>is their fear on his face? or is he emotionless and cold?</li> <li>is their panic expressed on his face or is he calculating and stoned faced?</li> <li>if he were to detonate a suicide vest, are you or others in immediate danger? or has everyone ran far enough that minimal loss of life would take place if he were to blow himself up? <ol> <li>if this is the case, give commands to keep his hands up in the air and stay where he is until authorities arrive or everyone is far enough away that he is no longer a threat to you or anyone else.</li> <li>depending on what he does next will give you a better understanding of what his intentions are, and whether or not you have to shoot.</li> </ol> </li> </ol> </li> </ol> <p>IMPORTANT: In these types of situations, chaos will ensue. People will be irrational and make many mistakes, including police and other possible concealed weapons holders. Although you are not the threat, you must understand that other people do not know this. YOU CAN BE MISTAKENLY SEEN AS THE THREAT, so you must do everything in your power to let everyone know you are one of the good guys.</p> <ol> <li>SCREAM LOAD VERBAL COMMANDS: make sure it is known exactly what your intentions are, by verbalizing everything you are doing load enough that everyone can hear you are attempting to protect them by trying to neutralize a suspected threat.</li> <li>TELL OTHERS TO CALL 911 AND TELL THE DISPATCHER YOU ARE THE GOOD GUY: do whatever you can to have someone dial 911 and make sure they tell the dispatcher exactly what is going on, and especially what you are wearing to avoid the police mistakenly thinking you are the threat. This might not be a feasible option with the panic happening all around you especially while you are making life or death decisions and scanning the area for additional threats. If possible dial 911 on your cell phone and put the phone somewhere that the dispatcher can hear your verbal commands. In between commands or whenever possible, scream “911 dispatcher I have the suspect at gun point, I am wearing a *whatever color shirt you are wearing* shirt, tell your officers I am not a threat and not to shoot, the suspect is wearing *describe the suspect* and I suspect he is wearing a suicide vest warn your officers to approach with caution” and repeat this saying over and over again, as loud as possible. You want everyone in the area to know exactly what your intentions are. This will increase the odds of you staying alive from other individuals carrying a firearm and the police when they arrive on the scene.</li> </ol> <p>This is where professional training makes the difference between life and death. Proper training will give you better insight on the&nbsp;difference between&nbsp;a an innocent civilian that is panicked and frozen with fear and a terrorist trying to murder innocent civilians and first responders. Seconds count, you have to be as prepared as possible for anything and everything. &nbsp;There is no training like this for civilians, concealed weapons holders do not have the ability to train for something like this, it just doesn’t exist. So it’s really up to you to train yourself to handle this type of situation.</p> <p><em><strong>Practice and proficiency with your firearm will build confidence and allow you to keep a level head in time of chaos.&nbsp;</strong></em></p> <p>One thing these terrorists did not anticipate is for <em><strong>all Americans to be armed and prepared</strong></em> to fight back at any given time, anywhere. The government has failed to protect us against enemies, foreign and domestic. &nbsp;It’s time to take your life into your own hands, and increase the odds in your favor.</p> <p>Although having a concealed weapon is one of the first steps in being prepared, simply carrying a firearm does not mean you are prepared to deal with this type of threat. I estimate 95% of concealed weapon permit holders would not perform well in this type of situation. This is no ones fault, remember, this is a new type of threat we are facing. With new threats comes new types of required training. The more training you familiarize your self with the better off you and the people around you will be.</p> <p>If you want more information on <strong>how to stay alive during a terrorist attack</strong> or would like to get professional firearms training, contact me and refuse to be a victim. You don’t have to be a statistic. It doesn’t matter your&nbsp;age, sex, weight, height or build. Anyone and everyone should and can become proficient with a firearm. You could be the only thing between one or more of these scumbags murdering you and everyone around you. You can and should be the person that has the ability to take out these fucking scumbag when seconds count&nbsp;in a life or death scenario. You have the choice to be the wolf or the sheep.&nbsp;I choose to be a wolf, I train to be a wolf, and when the time comes to act, I will be the wolf. What do you choose to be? The better question is: WHAT ARE YOU DOING TO BECOME THE WOLF YOU NEED TO BE TO STAY ALIVE?</p> </div> <p>Best Regards,<br> <strong>Matt Adika</strong><br> <em>Presdent</em><br> Florida Gun Classifieds<br> 11070 Wiles Rd.<br> Coral Springs, Fl. 33076<br> Tel:&nbsp; (954) 805-3440<br> Fax: (954) 227-2877<br> Email:&nbsp;<a title="Mailto matt@floridagunclassifieds.com" href="mailto:matt@floridagunclassifieds.com" target="_blank">matt@floridagunclassifieds.com</a><br> Website: <a title="Florida Gun Classifieds" href="http://floridagunclassifieds.com/" target="_blank">http://floridagunclassifieds.com</a><br> Online Store: <a href="http://floridagunclassifieds.com/online-gun-store" target="_blank">http://floridagunclassifieds.com/online-gun-store</a><br> <a class="cboxElement" href="http://i0.wp.com/sellgunsforcash.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/03/facebook-gunshot.png" data-rel="colorbox"><img src="http://i0.wp.com/sellgunsforcash.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/03/facebook-gunshot.png?resize=45%2C42" alt="facebook gunshot" width="45" height="42"></a>&nbsp;<a title="Facebook Florida Gun Classifieds" href="http://facebook.com/floridagunclassifieds" target="_blank">Like us!
