250w" sizes="(max-width: 150px) 100vw, 150px"> <h1 style="text-align: center;">Let us Custom Build AR15 SBR of your dreams!</h1> <p>I’ve always wanted bad ass Custom Build AR15 SBR, I’ve just been so busy I never got around to doing it. Well, lets just say an opportunity presented itself and a $300 lower turned into a $2500 bad ass Custom Build AR15 SBR.</p> <h3 style="text-align: center;">The video below describes the Custom Build AR15 SBR, and demonstrates how it shoots and the features.</h3> <h4 style="text-align: center;">Lets just say, It exceeded all my expectations and I was not disappointed. This Custom Build AR15 SBR was everything I wanted and more. It performed flawlessly. Florida Gun Classifieds specializes in custom work of all kinds. From building one of a kind Custom Build AR15 SBR’s, to Dura and Ceracoating exisiting rifles and pistols, whatever you need we can do!</h4> <p><iframe src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/oCy-38gaAw0" width="560" height="315" frameborder="0" allowfullscreen="allowfullscreen"></iframe></p> <p>Our Custom Build AR15 SBR used the following parts to make the beautiful piece of ART you see above.</p> <ul> <li>Spikes Tactical Hellbreaker Billet Lower</li> <li>SpecOp 4lbs Custom Billet Trigger</li> <li>SpecOp Billet Upper</li> <li>Blackhole Weaponry match grade 10.5″ barrel.</li> <li>Troy PWD telescopic stock w/ Troy BGC and buffer tube spring</li> <li>Sons of Liberty Gun Works SOLGW Mk10 Ultralite Rail 15″ DPMS Low Rail MLOK</li> <li>Adjustable Gas Block0</li> <li>Acog 4x Optic</li> <li>Magpul BUIS</li> <li>Huntertown Arms Kestrel 556 Suppressor</li> <li>Magpul Vertical Foregrip4Magpul 40 round Pmag</li> </ul> <p>We can guide you in the right direction and assist you in completing all the necessary paperwork to obtain a&nbsp;Class III NFA item.</p> <p>There are usually many questions regarding NFA items, Firearms Trusts and the DO’s and DON’Ts of owning a Class III firearm. Although I am not an attorney, and cannot answer legal questions, please feel free to contact me to discuss the process&nbsp;or answer any questions you may have about obtaining a Class III NFA Item to the best of my ability such as a Custom Build AR15 SBR, Suppressor or Full Auto Machine gun.</p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p><img src="http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/03/matt.jpg?resize=201%2C201" alt="matt"></p> <p>Best Regards,<br> <strong>Matt Adika</strong><br> <em>Presdent</em><br> Florida Gun Classifieds<br> 11070 Wiles Rd.<br> Coral Springs, Fl. 33076<br> Tel:&nbsp; (954) 805-3440<br> Fax: (954) 227-2877<br> Email:&nbsp;<a title="Mailto matt@floridagunclassifieds.com" href="mailto:matt@floridagunclassifieds.com" target="_blank">matt@floridagunclassifieds.com</a><br> Website: <a title="Florida Gun Classifieds" href="http://floridagunclassifieds.com/" target="_blank">http://floridagunclassifieds.com</a><br> Online Store: <a href="http://floridagunclassifieds.com/online-gun-store" target="_blank">http://floridagunclassifieds.com/online-gun-store</a><br> <a class="cboxElement" href="http://i0.wp.com/sellgunsforcash.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/03/facebook-gunshot.png" data-rel="colorbox"><img src="http://i0.wp.com/sellgunsforcash.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/03/facebook-gunshot.png?zoom=1.5&amp;resize=45%2C42" srcset="http://i0.wp.com/sellgunsforcash.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/03/facebook-gunshot.png?zoom=1.5&amp;resize=45%2C42" alt="facebook gunshot" width="45" height="42"></a>&nbsp;<a title="Facebook Florida Gun Classifieds" href="http://facebook.com/floridagunclassifieds" target="_blank">Like us! class="shadowblock_out post-13098 post type-post status-publish format-standard has-post-thumbnail hentry category-firearms-blog" id="post-13098"> <div class="shadowblock"> <div class="dashicons-before comment-bubble"><a href="http://floridagunclassifieds.com/terror-suspects-legally-purchased-guns/#respond" class="bubble cp-fixed-color">0</a></div> <h3 class="loop"><a href="http://floridagunclassifieds.com/terror-suspects-legally-purchased-guns/" title="Terror suspects legally purchased guns in the United States from 2004 to 2014">Terror suspects legally purchased guns in the United States from 2004 to 2014</a></h3> <p class="meta dotted"><span class="dashicons-before user"><a href="http://floridagunclassifieds.com/author/matt-adika/" title="Posts by Matt Adika" rel="author">Matt Adika</a></span> <span class="dashicons-before folderb"><a href="http://floridagunclassifieds.com/category/firearms-blog/" rel="category tag">Firearms Blog</a></span> <span class="dashicons-before clock"><span>November 22, 2015</span></span></p> <div class="entry-content"> <img width="150" height="103" src="http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/11/isis.jpg?fit=150%2C103" class="attachment-blog-thumbnail size-blog-thumbnail wp-post-image" alt="Terror suspects legally purchased guns" srcset="http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/11/isis.jpg?w=670 670w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/11/isis.jpg?resize=50%2C34 50w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/11/isis.jpg?resize=200%2C137 200w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/11/isis.jpg?resize=500%2C343 500w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/11/isis.jpg?resize=100%2C69 100w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/11/isis.jpg?resize=150%2C103 150w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/11/isis.jpg?resize=440%2C300 440w" sizes="(max-width: 150px) 100vw, 150px"> <h1 style="text-align: center;">Terror suspects legally purchased guns in the United States from 2004 to 2014 says FBI</h1> <p>This statement was taken from a new FBI study that was recently released. Now when hearing something like this, your immediate reaction might be to scream “WHAT THE F*#&amp;$?” and take your computer screen and throw it at the TV while Nancy Pelosi is squawking about gun violence and global warming on CSPAN, but lets think about this for a minute……</p> <h2>Ask you self, how many of these so called “terrorists” used these legally purchased guns in any kind of attack against anyone let alone US citizens. The answer is ZERO. None of these guns have and will ever be used in any terrorist attack, because these bullshit statistics are nothing more then a scare tactic to make you and everyone else so terrified of guns that it forces you to side with the anti-gunners and make a quick and rash decision to pass some kind of pointless gun legislation that will restrict law abiding gun owners from practicing their 2nd amendment right to bear arms.</h2> <p>Read this bullshit article below and remember that “terrorists”, criminals or anyone with the intent to do harm to someone, can get firearms, knifes, cars, baseball bats, or anything else that be used as a weapon anywhere. New legislation regarding legal gun purchases and ownership will not stop evil from obtaining anything ever, let alone firearms.</p> <h3>Last time I checked drugs were&nbsp;illegal, but drug abuse is one of the largest problems facing our country today. We have harsh penalties for the possession and distribution of these illegal drugs, but don’t have the same vigorous attitude toward rehabilitation and treatment for our own people who have fallen into the trap of this deadly disease. America is quick to punish people for breaking the law, but then gives no solution to combating the problem and helping its citizens to avoid repeating the same mistake over and over and keeping them out of jail or worse, death.</h3> <h4>This is the same concept they are trying to push on us with gun control. Lets ban all guns now! which translates to this: Once law abiding citizens are banned from purchasing or possessing firearms, then what will happen? Will crime automatically drop? will murders decrease? will school shooting be a thing of the past?</h4> <p>Unfortunately NO!</p> <p>because these politicians forgot one major thing….</p> <p style="font-size: 200%; text-align: center;"><strong>CRIMINALS DON’T FOLLOW LAWS!</strong></p> <p>Given France’s strict gun laws, the&nbsp;terrorists who attacked Paris on Friday may have&nbsp;<a href="http://www.thedailybeast.com/articles/2015/11/13/this-is-how-ak-47s-get-to-paris.html" target="_blank">turned to black market sources</a> for the weapons they used. But in the United States, known and suspected terrorists are allowed to purchase firearms under federal law.</p> <p>“Membership in a terrorist organization does not prohibit a person from possessing firearms or explosives under current federal law,” the Government Accountability Office concluded in 2010. The&nbsp;law prohibits&nbsp;felons, fugitives, drug addicts and domestic abusers from <a href="http://smartgunlaws.org/prohibited-people-gun-purchaser-policy-summary/" target="_blank">purchasing a firearm in the United States</a>. But people on <a href="https://www.fbi.gov/about-us/nsb/tsc" target="_blank">the FBI’s consolidated terrorist watchlist</a>&nbsp;— typically placed there when there is “<a href="https://www.fbi.gov/about-us/nsb/tsc/terrorist-screening-center-frequently-asked-questions" target="_blank">reasonable suspicion</a>” that they are a known or suspected terrorist&nbsp;— can freely purchase handguns or assault-style rifles.&nbsp;Terror suspects legally purchased guns.</p> <p>And, as the GAO found, a number of them do:&nbsp;Terror suspects legally purchased guns. Between 2004 and 2014,&nbsp;suspected terrorists attempted to purchase guns from American dealers at least 2,233 times. And in 2,043 of those cases&nbsp;— 91 percent of the time&nbsp;— they succeeded. There are about 700,000 people on the watch-list&nbsp;— a point that civil libertarians have made to underscore that many on the list may be&nbsp;family members or acquaintances of people with potential terrorist connections.</p> <div class="inline-content inline-photo inline-photo-normal horizontal-photo modal-1"><a name="104857b948"></a><img class="courtesy-of-the-resizer zoom-in alignnone" src="https://img.washingtonpost.com/wp-apps/imrs.php?src=https://img.washingtonpost.com/blogs/wonkblog/files/2015/11/terror-guns.png&amp;w=1484" alt="Terror suspects legally purchased guns" width="1484" height="1392" data-hi-res-src="https://img.washingtonpost.com/wp-apps/imrs.php?src=https://img.washingtonpost.com/blogs/wonkblog/files/2015/11/terror-guns.png&amp;w=1484" data-low-res-src="https://img.washingtonpost.com/wp-apps/imrs.php?src=https://img.washingtonpost.com/blogs/wonkblog/files/2015/11/terror-guns.png&amp;w=480"></div> <p>That total number is a floor,&nbsp;since the 2011 and 2012 numbers include only partial data because of a programming error that the FBI subsequently fixed, according to the GAO. Overall,&nbsp;looking back toward 2007,&nbsp;the annual number of attempted gun purchases by terror suspects has generally held steady and may be declining slightly year-over-year.</p> <p>Lawmakers have tried to stop Terror suspects legally purchased guns from happening. Bills have been introduced in Congress to do just that, going as far back as 2007 at the behest of then-Attorney General Alberto Gonzales.</p> <p>Sen. Dianne Feinstein (D-Calif.) and Rep. Peter T. King (R-N.Y.) introduced a bill to do that earlier this year. The “<a href="http://www.feinstein.senate.gov/public/index.cfm/files/serve/?File_id=e0e0dab0-d7d7-4dca-83da-7b68f5be2b47" target="_blank">Denying Firearms and Explosives to Dangerous Terrorists Act of 2015</a>” would prevent Terror suspects legally purchased guns several hundred gun purchases by suspected terrorists each year, and it includes provisions to let people challenge a denial if they believe they were placed on the watch list in error.</p> <p>But these bills have&nbsp;rarely made it out of committee, in part due to vehement opposition from the National Rifle Association&nbsp;and its allies in Congress. The NRA <a href="https://www.nraila.org/articles/20110419/why-nra-opposes-gun-control-supporters" target="_blank">objected to earlier versions of the bill</a>, saying they were “aimed primarily at law-abiding American gun owners,” that “prohibiting the possession of firearms doesn’t stop criminals from illegally acquiring them,” and that the bills were “sponsored by gun control extremists.”</p> <p>I reached out to the NRA to find out if they were similarly opposed to this year’s Feinstein/King bill but they have not yet responded. This piece will be updated if&nbsp;they do. &nbsp;A 2012 survey conducted by conservative pollster Frank Luntz, for pro-gun-control group Everytown USA, found that 76 percent of American gun owners, including 71 percent of NRA members, supported prohibiting people on the terror watch list from buying guns.</p> <p>The biggest knock against the proposed legislation is perhaps that the FBI’s watch list is an imperfect tool for assessing an individual’s terror threat. Civil libertarians <a href="https://theintercept.com/2014/08/05/watch-commander/" target="_blank">warn</a> that the watch list has ballooned in size to nearly 700,000 individuals in recent years. Many of those people may simply be family members, acquaintances or people only marginally acquainted with individuals who actually belong to terror groups. The NRA and its allies are worried that perfectly law-abiding people may end up on a watch list and be unable to purchase a gun.</p> <p>No one is against Terrorists purchasing firearms, but show me one incident where these so called Terror suspects legally purchased guns and used them against american citizens in a terror attack. IT DOESN’T EXIST. Criminals don’t purchase guns legally, just like drugs they turn to the black market to get these weapons to kill.</p> <div class="sharedaddy sd-sharing-enabled"><div class="robots-nocontent sd-block class="shadowblock_out post-12221 post type-post status-publish format-standard has-post-thumbnail hentry category-firearms-blog" id="post-12221"> <div class="shadowblock"> <div class="dashicons-before comment-bubble"><a href="http://floridagunclassifieds.com/gun-control-conspiracy/#respond" class="bubble cp-fixed-color">0</a></div> <h3 class="loop"><a href="http://floridagunclassifieds.com/gun-control-conspiracy/" title="Gun Control Conspiracy – An FFL’s Perspective on things">Gun Control Conspiracy – An FFL’s Perspective on things</a></h3> <p class="meta dotted"><span class="dashicons-before user"><a href="http://floridagunclassifieds.com/author/matt-adika/" title="Posts by Matt Adika" rel="author">Matt Adika</a></span> <span class="dashicons-before folderb"><a href="http://floridagunclassifieds.com/category/firearms-blog/" rel="category tag">Firearms Blog</a></span> <span class="dashicons-before clock"><span>October 8, 2015</span></span></p> <div class="entry-content"> <img width="150" height="84" src="http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/10/ObamaSpyPIX-420x215.jpg?fit=150%2C84" class="attachment-blog-thumbnail size-blog-thumbnail wp-post-image" alt="4473 government" srcset="http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/10/ObamaSpyPIX-420x215.jpg?w=518 518w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/10/ObamaSpyPIX-420x215.jpg?resize=50%2C28 50w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/10/ObamaSpyPIX-420x215.jpg?resize=200%2C112 200w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/10/ObamaSpyPIX-420x215.jpg?resize=500%2C279 500w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/10/ObamaSpyPIX-420x215.jpg?resize=100%2C56 100w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/10/ObamaSpyPIX-420x215.jpg?resize=150%2C84 150w" sizes="(max-width: 150px) 100vw, 150px"> <h1 style="text-align: center;">Gun Control Conspiracy</h1> <h2 style="text-align: center;">Does the government know which guns are bought from a licensed firearms dealer?</h2> <p>There is more misinformation and debate regarding &nbsp;this&nbsp;Gun Control Conspiracy then any other gun related conspiracy theory out there. This Gun Control Conspiracy, which is brought up often on social media and always seems to get everyone pretty fired up, makes some individuals so worried they won’t even step foot into a firearms store.</p> <h3 style="text-align: center;"><em><strong>As a Federal Firearms Licensed Dealer, I am writing this article to discuss the common misconceptions regarding this Gun Control Conspiracy, and what happens the information you disclose when you fill out the form 4473 background check paperwork that is required to purchase any firearm in America from a FFL Dealer.</strong></em></h3> <p><img class="aligncenter wp-image-12226 size-large" src="http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/10/Form-4473.jpg?resize=500%2C287" alt="gun control conspiracy" srcset="http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/10/Form-4473.jpg?resize=500%2C287 500w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/10/Form-4473.jpg?resize=50%2C29 50w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/10/Form-4473.jpg?resize=200%2C115 200w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/10/Form-4473.jpg?resize=100%2C57 100w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/10/Form-4473.jpg?resize=150%2C86 150w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/10/Form-4473.jpg?w=600 600w" sizes="(max-width: 500px) 100vw, 500px" data-recalc-dims="1"></p> <p>Form 4473 is the standard form that <em><strong>everyone</strong></em> must fill out in order to purchase a firearm in the United States. Before any person leaves the store with any firearm, regardless of the type, caliber or purpose, each individual must complete the form completely, accurately and also testify that the information on the form is truthful to the best of their knowledge. The front asks basic information such as Name, address, place of birth, height, weight, sex, birth date, as well as 15 pre-qualification questions which could immediately disqualify the buyer if answered incorrectly. Some of these questions include “have you ever been convicted in of a felony?” and “are you a fugitive from justice?” <strong><em>Any person with even the slightest bit of common sense can figure out how to answer these questions correctly to pass to the next stage of the process</em></strong>, which is the dealer taking the information from the 4473 and inputting it into the state run background check system which in Florida is run by FDLE, or Florida Department if Law Enforcement. The dealer submits the information provided, checks the ID and or CWP of the buyer and waits for a response. This is done for every single firearm sold, every single time a transaction takes place. Once the transaction is complete, if you walk out of the door of the FFL and decide to come back 5 seconds later and buy another gun, by law another 4473 must be completed and the background check must be ran again.</p> <h4 style="text-align: center;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;"><em><strong>There is a huge misconception that anyone can just walk into a gun store and walk out with a firearm without any oversight at all. This is completely 100% FALSE and feeds into the&nbsp;Gun Control Conspiracy narrative.</strong></em></span></h4> <h4><em><strong>The only people legally allowed to purchase a firearm and leave the same day requires three things. </strong></em></h4> <ol> <li><em><strong>#1 We must get an approval response from FDLE letting the dealer know the person is not a felon</strong></em></li> <li><em><strong>#2 the customer must have a valid Florida Drivers License and </strong></em></li> <li><em><strong>#3 the customer must have a Concealed Weapons Permit. </strong></em></li> </ol> <p>The only exception to these three requirements is that if the customer is approved and trades in a firearm, he only has to be a Florida resident, he does not have to have a concealed weapons permit. The customer may trade a pistol for a pistol and/or a rifle for a rifle only. Logic behind this is that if that person was interested in committing some type of crime why not just use the firearm he already has in his possession? Trading the firearm in for a new gun will not have any effect on the outcome of the situation, <em><strong>although to this date I can not find any instances where a law abiding citizen with no criminal history traded in a firearm in Florida for the sole purpose of obtaining a new firearm to commit a crime</strong></em>. Keep in mind the background check must still <strong>ALWAYS BE RUN</strong>. The&nbsp;anti-gun left wants you to think buying a gun is a free for all…. its not..&nbsp;The law here actually works and makes sense.</p> <h4 style="text-align: center;"><em><strong>What information is actually given to FDLE when my FFL does my background? </strong></em></h4> <p><img class="alignleft wp-image-12227" src="http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/10/gun-control-ng.jpg?resize=341%2C231" alt="gun control conspiracy" srcset="http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/10/gun-control-ng.jpg?resize=500%2C339 500w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/10/gun-control-ng.jpg?resize=50%2C34 50w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/10/gun-control-ng.jpg?resize=200%2C136 200w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/10/gun-control-ng.jpg?resize=100%2C68 100w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/10/gun-control-ng.jpg?resize=150%2C102 150w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/10/gun-control-ng.jpg?w=600 600w" sizes="(max-width: 341px) 100vw, 341px" data-recalc-dims="1"></p> <p><em><strong>The FFL only inputs the data from the 4473 that can identify you from someone else.</strong></em> Full Name, Suffix, State of residence, Place of Birth, Sex, Race, and Social Security Number which is optional. That’s it ladies and gentlemen. So now&nbsp;we know what information is being transmitted to FDLE, and the only thing that’s being submitted is identifying information to verify you are who you say you are, so right from the beginning there is no information on the firearm being purchased ever being submitted to any government agency at the time of the transaction. <em><strong>The only time any Make, Model or Serial numbers are submitted to the ATF and Local Law Enforcement is when there is a multiple handgun purchase of one or more handguns purchased within a 5 day period.</strong></em> If this occurs the FFL must complete a multiple sale form and list all the pistols that were sold to that individual along with name, address, DL #, Place of birth and other identifying information. This is so if someone walks into a store and buys 10 Glock 19’s, unless there teaching a firearms class or buying arms for their police department, the ATF wants to make sure that those firearms are not being purchased strictly to resell on the black market for a profit. Don’t be afraid to purchase more than one firearm, as long as you are not doing anything illegal there is nothing to worry about. You could also spread the purchases over a 7 day period so no multiple paperwork even has to be filed. &nbsp;<em><strong>There is no way the government could know every gun that a law abiding citizen purchases from a FFL Dealer</strong></em>. Although the FFL is required to fill out the 4473 with the Make, Model, Serial # and Caliber of the firearm, as well as certify that the disposition has taken place on that specific date. The firearm is then logged out of the Aquisition and Disposition book to the customer who was approved by FDLE. The FFL Dealer then takes the 4473 and is required to keep the original in a secure location for 20 years. Although from time to time we will get a call from the ATF Tracing Center trying to locate a particular firearm. They request details regarding specific firearms and ask who those firearms were sold to. <strong><em>This is extremely rare and only occurs when a firearm is found at the scene of a crime and they are trying to track down the last known owner to get some answers as so how they found their firearm at the scene.</em></strong> Most of the time, that person has already sold that firearm to owner #2, who sold it to owner #3, who let his brother #4 borrow it, who filed a police report the week prior about someone breaking into his car and stealing his brother’s gun.</p> <h4><em><strong><img class="alignright wp-image-12228 size-medium" src="http://i1.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/10/domestic-drone-cartoon.jpg?resize=200%2C125" alt="gun control conspiracy" srcset="http://i1.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/10/domestic-drone-cartoon.jpg?resize=200%2C125 200w, http://i1.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/10/domestic-drone-cartoon.jpg?resize=50%2C31 50w, http://i1.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/10/domestic-drone-cartoon.jpg?resize=500%2C313 500w, http://i1.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/10/domestic-drone-cartoon.jpg?resize=100%2C63 100w, http://i1.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/10/domestic-drone-cartoon.jpg?resize=150%2C94 150w, http://i1.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/10/domestic-drone-cartoon.jpg?w=600 600w" sizes="(max-width: 200px) 100vw, 200px" data-recalc-dims="1">The idea that the government is behind this Gun Control Conspiracy and knows each and every firearm purchased on a daily basis and by whom that firearm is purchased by is 100% FALSE and technically impossible to implement with the current system.</strong></em></h4> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p>Think about this…. When inputting the customers identifying information, if we were required to also enter in the firearm serial # for example, and then that customer came back declined because of a past criminal charge, what happens to that firearm in the database? Does the customer now own that gun? what if he is a conditional non approval which takes more then five days to return a response? How would that work? What about a Non-Approval? How would they know which gun he ended up with if he was Approved after the 21 day appeal process to ensure he can legally own the firearm because there is some sort of discrepancy.</p> <p><em><strong>Let’s be clear about something: <span style="color: #000000;">AT NO TIME DOES ANY SERIAL NUMBER EVER GET RELAYED OR TRANSMITTED TO FDLE OR THE ATF AT THE TIME OF THE SALE.</span></strong> </em></p> <p>So all of you anti FFL guys can rest easy, you can actually buy a new gun from a firearms store without having to look over your shoulder for Obama to come and confiscate your firearms.</p> <h4 style="text-align: center;"><em><strong>Is&nbsp;there a National Registry for firearms where every gun is registered to a particular owner? 100% FALSE Gun Control Conspiracy.</strong></em></h4> <p>The only thing linking the firearm you purchase from a FFL dealer to yourself is the 4473 you filled out and the dealer filled out, which is usually sitting inside a filing cabinet in the back of the store somewhere for years at a time. <strong><em>Occasionally the ATF will call and ask who the firearm was sold to, but in the last 4 years of selling firearms to over 3000 people, I can count on one hand how many times I received that phone call.</em></strong> Now I know what some of you Anti-FFL Pro-Private sale guys are going to say. “But if the government really wanted to, they could go into every FFL dealer in the country and demand them to hand over every 4473 they have for the last 20 years.” And you would be right. This is a possibility, but lets think about that for a second. There are approximetly 50,000 Federal Firearms Licensed Dealers in the country give or take. I’m sure the amount of firearms sold ranges from 1 per year to 100,000 per year depending on what type of business it is. I have own a small firearms store in South Florida, and I sell an average of 1000 guns per year. So lets use that number to figure out how many guns are sold each year as a rough estimate, which will tell us how many 4473 there has to be throughout the country. 50,000 x 1000 = that’s 500,000 4473 ‘s per year and now lets multiply that by 20 years which is the time the FFL is required to keep all 4473’s = <em><strong>10,0000 million 4473’s were filled out and stuffed in a filing cabinet over the last 20 years.</strong></em> 10,000,000 4 page documents, all with chicken scratch from not only the customer, but the FFL who fills these things out by the thousands per year, which each one done as the day goes on gets sloppier and sloppier to the point where when you review your paperwork for the day you say to yourself <em><strong>“what the fuck does that say?”</strong></em> <img class="alignleft wp-image-12229" src="http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/10/Paperwork.gif?resize=237%2C237" alt="gun control conspiracy" srcset="http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/10/Paperwork.gif?resize=150%2C150 150w, http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/10/Paperwork.gif?resize=50%2C50 50w, http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/10/Paperwork.gif?resize=250%2C250 250w" sizes="(max-width: 237px) 100vw, 237px" data-recalc-dims="1">after severe carpal tunnel syndrome from writing so much day in and day out, the FFL then takes all his hard work, and hands it over to the government of the great USA as part of the Gun Control Conspiracy, <strong><em>who cant even implement a health care marketplace correctly</em></strong>, which is basically a website where you can see which health insurance plans are available in your state (I could have made that website in a week. &nbsp;So you tell me if they could take 10,000,000 4473’s (who knows what the real number is i’m sure its quadruple that) and transcribe the hand written chicken scratch into usable data in a database where it can then be turned over to a military team to target <strong>YOU</strong>.</p> <h4 style="text-align: center;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;"><em><strong>Now lets remember who YOU are……..<img class="aligncenter wp-image-12230 " src="http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/10/should-average-joes-be-president.jpg?resize=210%2C319" alt="gun control conspiracy" srcset="http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/10/should-average-joes-be-president.jpg?w=281 281w, http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/10/should-average-joes-be-president.jpg?resize=33%2C50 33w, http://i2.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/10/should-average-joes-be-president.jpg?resize=66%2C100 66w" sizes="(max-width: 210px) 100vw, 210px" data-recalc-dims="1"></strong></em></span></h4> <p>Joe Shmo, who is a member of 73 gun enthusiast groups on facebook, posts anti-Obama memes all over his facebook wall, likes every page recommended to him that has anything to do with 2nd amendment, guns, freedom, liberty, has a chick with big tits holding a gun in the profile pic, it doesn’t matter what it is <em><strong>as long as its red, white and blue and&nbsp;related&nbsp;to guns, you are BOUT THAT GUN LIFE</strong></em>, with your new profile pic which just recently has been updated to a video of you shooting a fully automatic AR-15 while the picture above has a picture of your safe with about 15 or so firearms, all while you constantly buying and selling guns on every group, forum and website ever created online.</p> <h5><em><strong>So you tell me, what is more likely to happen…<img class="alignright wp-image-12231 size-full" src="http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/10/Camp-FEMA-300x225.jpg?resize=300%2C225" alt="gun control conspiracy" srcset="http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/10/Camp-FEMA-300x225.jpg?resize=300%2C225 300w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/10/Camp-FEMA-300x225.jpg?resize=50%2C38 50w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/10/Camp-FEMA-300x225.jpg?resize=200%2C150 200w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/10/Camp-FEMA-300x225.jpg?resize=100%2C75 100w, http://i0.wp.com/floridagunclassifieds.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/10/Camp-FEMA-300x225.jpg?resize=150%2C113 150w" sizes="(max-width: 300px) 100vw, 300px" data-recalc-dims="1"></strong></em></h5> <p>A Huge Gun Control Conspiracy in which government agents secretly visit every gun shop in America every month and record the names and addresses and&nbsp;guns that you purchased legally in a secret database so when President Obama decides to declare martial law they will know which house to hit first to seize every gun in America leaving you defenseless and thrown into a FEMA camp to die.</p>
